# <a name="hololens-2-release-notes"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-103">HoloLens 2 发行说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-103">HoloLens 2 release notes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-104">若要确保你的 HoloLens 设备具有工作效率，我们将继续发布功能、bug 和安全更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-104">To ensure you have a productive experience with your HoloLens devices, we continue to release feature, bug, and security updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-105">在此页上，可以查看每个月 HoloLens 的新增功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-105">On this page, you can see what’s new for HoloLens each month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-106">若要获取最新的 HoloLens 2 更新，可以[检查更新并手动更新](hololens-update-hololens.md#check-for-updates-and-manually-update)或获取完全更新， (FFU) [通过高级恢复助理来闪存设备](hololens-recovery.md#clean-reflash-the-device)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-106">To get the latest HoloLens 2 update, you can either [check for updates and manually update](hololens-update-hololens.md#check-for-updates-and-manually-update) or get the Full Flash Update (FFU) to [flash your device via Advanced Recovery Companion](hololens-recovery.md#clean-reflash-the-device).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-107">[下载](https://aka.ms/hololens2download)内容保持最新，并提供最新的公开发布版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-107">The [download](https://aka.ms/hololens2download) is kept up to date and provides the latest generally available build.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-108">最近的 Windows 11 公告重点介绍 Windows 的 PC 版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-108">The recent Windows 11 announcement was focused on the PC version of Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-109">我们最近在5月2021推出了一个 HoloLens 2 的[主要 OS 更新](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/mixed-reality-blog/what-s-new-in-windows-holographic-version-21h1/ba-p/2337067)，我们将根据客户对此秋季的反馈来处理即将发布的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-109">We recently launched a [major OS update](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/mixed-reality-blog/what-s-new-in-windows-holographic-version-21h1/ba-p/2337067) to HoloLens 2 in May 2021, and we are working on an upcoming release based on customer feedback for this fall.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-110">由于现已解决[了21H1 内部版本中影响远程协助用户的已知问题](hololens-troubleshooting.md#remote-assist-video-freezes-after-20-minutes)，我们暂时暂停了 Windows 全息版21H1 更新的产品/服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-110">Due to a now resolved [known issue in our 21H1 build that was affecting Remote Assist users](hololens-troubleshooting.md#remote-assist-video-freezes-after-20-minutes), we temporally paused the offering of Windows Holographic, version 21H1 updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-111">我们还更改了默认的高级恢复助理 (ARC) 生成到[Windows 全息，版本20H2 –2021年6月更新](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2--june-2021-update)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-111">We had also changed the default Advanced Recovery Companion (ARC) build to the [Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – June 2021 Update](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2--june-2021-update).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-112">现在，圆弧生成将恢复为21H1 生成的目标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-112">The ARC build will now resume targeting the 21H1 build.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-21h1---july-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-113">Windows21H1 版本-2021 年7月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-113">Windows Holographic, version 21H1 - July 2021 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-114">生成20348.1010</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-114">Build 20348.1010</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-115">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-115">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-116">当文件资源管理器在打开锁定的文件时遇到问题时，设备门户已增强了通知客户的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-116">Device Portal has enhanced methods of notifying the customer when File Explorer encounters issues opening locked files.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-117">如果使用的是集成和离散图形适配器的 PC 上的 HoloLens 2 Emulator，则在大多数情况下，模拟器现在能够启用硬件图形加速，尽管它可能会使用功能不太强大的集成适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-117">When using the HoloLens 2 Emulator on a PC with both integrated and discrete graphics adapters, the emulator will, in most cases, now be able to enable hardware graphics acceleration, though it might use the less powerful integrated adapter.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-118">以前，无法启用硬件加速，通常使用代码43报告图形故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-118">Previously, hardware acceleration could not be enabled, often reporting a graphics failure with Code 43.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-119">在某些情况下，仿真程序将不会成功启动，而是立即启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-119">In some cases, the emulator would not boot successfully but now will.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-120">在所有受支持的浏览器中使用 https 时，文件上载、下载、重命名和删除现已修复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-120">File upload, download, rename and delete is now fixed when using https in all supported browsers.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-121">修复了从设置 > 网络启动 Wi-Fi 属性 UI 时无法保存 Wi-Fi 代理 **& > > 状态的** 问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-121">Fixed issue where Wi-Fi proxy can't be saved when Wi-Fi properties UI is launched from **Settings -> Network & Internet -> Status -> Properties**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-122">解决了跨 OS 更新删除 eSIM 证书的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-122">Addressed an issue around the removal of eSIM certificates across OS updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-123">此修补程序可确保在更新到21H1 版本时删除 eSIM 证书和相关组件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-123">This fix ensures that the eSIM certificates and related components are removed when updating to the 21H1 release.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-124">更正了影响操作系统重置的预安装应用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-124">Corrected an issue impacting preinstalled apps across OS resets.</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-125">在增加 CPU 负载时，经过调整以增加运行时的电池充电性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-125">Battery charging performance tuned to increase runtime when charging with increased CPU loading.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-20h2--july-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-126">Windows版本20H2 –2021年7月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-126">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – July 2021 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-127">生成19041.1157</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-127">Build 19041.1157</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-128">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-128">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-129">当文件资源管理器在打开锁定的文件时遇到问题时，设备门户已增强了通知客户的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-129">Device Portal has enhanced methods of notifying the customer when File Explorer encounters issues opening locked files.</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-130">如果使用的是集成和离散图形适配器的 PC 上的 HoloLens 2 Emulator，则在大多数情况下，模拟器现在能够启用硬件图形加速，尽管它可能会使用功能不太强大的集成适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-130">When using the HoloLens 2 Emulator on a PC with both integrated and discrete graphics adapters, the emulator will, in most cases, now be able to enable hardware graphics acceleration, though it might use the less powerful integrated adapter.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-131">以前，无法启用硬件加速，通常使用代码43报告图形故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-131">Previously, hardware acceleration could not be enabled, often reporting a graphics failure with Code 43.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-132">在某些情况下，仿真程序将不会成功启动，而是立即启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-132">In some cases, the emulator would not boot successfully, but now will.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-133">在所有受支持的浏览器中使用 https 时，文件上载、下载、重命名和删除现已修复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-133">File upload, download, rename and delete is now fixed when using https in all supported browsers.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-21h1---june-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-134">Windows全息版 21H1-2021 年6月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-134">Windows Holographic, version 21H1 - June 2021 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-135">生成20348.1007</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-135">Build 20348.1007</span></span>

### <a name="onedrive-for-work-or-school-camera-roll-upload"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-136">OneDrive 工作或学校相机滚动上传</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-136">OneDrive for work or school Camera Roll upload</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-137">我们已向 HoloLens 2 设置应用添加了一项新功能，该功能使客户能够将混合现实照片和视频从设备的照片 > 照相机滚动文件夹自动上载到工作或学校文件夹的相应 OneDrive。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-137">We've added a new feature to the HoloLens 2 Settings app, which allows customers to automatically upload mixed reality photos and videos from the device's Pictures > Camera Roll folder to the corresponding OneDrive for work or school folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-138">此功能解决了 HoloLens 2 上[的 OneDrive 应用内的功能间隙](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#share-your-mixed-reality-photos-and-videos)，该功能仅支持将自动相机滚动更新到客户的个人 Microsoft 帐户 (而不支持其工作或学校帐户) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-138">This feature addresses a [feature gap within the OneDrive app](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#share-your-mixed-reality-photos-and-videos) on HoloLens 2, which only supports automatic Camera Roll upload to a customer's personal Microsoft account (and not their work or school account).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-139">**工作原理**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-139">**How it works**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-140">请访问 **设置 > 系统 > 混合现实相机**，以启用 "相机上传"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-140">Visit **Settings > System > Mixed Reality Camera** to enable "Camera upload."</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-141">如果将此功能设置为 "**开**" 位置，则捕获到你的设备的所有混合现实照片或视频都将自动排队，以便上传到工作或学校帐户的 OneDrive > 照相机滚动文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-141">By setting this feature to the **On** position, any mixed reality photos or videos captured to your device will automatically be queued for upload to the Pictures > Camera Roll folder of your OneDrive for work or school account.</span></span>
    >[!NOTE]
    ><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-142">在启用此功能之前捕获的照片和视频 *不* 会排队等待上载，但仍需手动上传。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-142">Photos and videos captured prior to enabling this feature *will not* be queued for upload and will still need to be manually uploaded.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-143">"设置" 页上的状态消息将显示等待上传的文件数 (或读取 "OneDrive 是最新的) "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-143">A status message on the Settings page will display the number of files pending upload (or read "OneDrive is up to date" when all pending files have been uploaded).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-144">如果你担心带宽或出于任何原因要 "暂停" 上载，则可以将该功能切换到 " **关闭** " 位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-144">If you're concerned about bandwidth or want to "pause" upload for any reason, you can switch the feature to the **Off** position.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-145">临时禁用该功能可确保在将新文件添加到 "相机照片" 文件夹中时，上传队列将继续增加，但在重新启用该功能之前，将不会上载文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-145">Temporarily disabling the feature ensures that the upload queue will continue to increase as you add new files to the Camera Roll folder, but files will not upload until you re-enable the feature.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-146">最新文件将首先上传 (最后一个) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-146">Newest files will upload first (last in, first out).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-147">如果 OneDrive 帐户有问题 (例如，更改密码后) "**立即修复**" 按钮将显示在 "设置" 页上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-147">If your OneDrive account has issues (for example, after your password changes) a **Fix now** button will appear on the Settings page.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-148">没有最大文件大小，但请注意，大文件上传会花费较长的时间，尤其是当上传带宽受到限制) 时 (。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-148">There is no maximum file size, but note that large files will take longer to upload (especially if your upload bandwidth is constrained).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-149">如果在上传大型文件时 "暂停" 或关闭上载，将保留部分上传。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-149">If you "pause" or turn off upload while a large file is being uploaded, the partial upload will be preserved.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-150">如果在 "已暂停" 或关闭的几个小时内重新启用上传，则上传将从中断的位置继续。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-150">If upload is re-enabled within several hours of being "paused" or turned off, the upload will continue from where it left off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-151">但是，如果在几个小时后重新启用上传，将从头开始重新启动大文件上传。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-151">However, if upload is re-enabled after several hours, the large file's upload will restart from the beginning.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-152">**已知问题和注意事项**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-152">**Known issues and caveats**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-153">此设置没有基于当前带宽使用情况的内置限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-153">This setting has no built in throttling based on current bandwidth usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-154">如果需要将其他方案的带宽最大化，请手动关闭该设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-154">If you need to maximize bandwidth for another scenario, turn off the setting manually.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-155">Upload 将暂停，但该功能将继续监视新添加到摄像卷筒中的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-155">Upload will be paused but the feature will continue to monitor newly added files to Camera Roll.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-156">准备就绪后，请重新启用上传。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-156">Re-enable upload when you're ready for it to continue.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-157">必须为设备上的每个用户帐户启用此功能，并且只能为当前已登录到设备的用户主动上载文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-157">This feature must be enabled for each user account on the device, and it can only actively upload files for the user who is currently signed-in to the device.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-158">如果你正在拍摄照片或视频，同时在设置页面上实时观看上传计数，请注意，在完成当前文件上传之前，挂起的文件数可能不会更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-158">If you're taking photos or videos while watching the upload count on the Settings page in real-time, note that the pending file count may not change until the current file has completed uploading.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-159">如果设备处于睡眠状态还是已关闭，Upload 将暂停。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-159">Upload will pause if your device falls asleep or is powered off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-160">若要确保等待的上载完成，请主动使用该设备，直到设置页面读取 "OneDrive 是最新的"，或调整 **Power & 睡眠** 设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-160">To ensure your pending uploads complete, actively use the device until the Settings page reads "OneDrive is up to date" or adjust your **Power & sleep** settings.</span></span>
### <a name="added-support-for-some-telemetry-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-161">添加了对某些遥测策略的支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-161">Added support for some telemetry policies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-162">HoloLens 2 上现在支持以下遥测策略：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-162">The following telemetry policies are now supported on the HoloLens 2:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-163">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-163">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-164">DisableDeviceDelete</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-164">DisableDeviceDelete</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-165">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-165">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-166">FeedbackHubAlwaysSaveDiagnosticsLocally</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-166">FeedbackHubAlwaysSaveDiagnosticsLocally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-167">System\AllowTelemetry 和 System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx 都应该一起使用，以便对设置应用程序中的遥测和行为具有完全控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-167">Both System\AllowTelemetry and System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx should be used together to have complete control on the Telemetry and behavior in the Settings app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-168">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-168">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-169">修复了颜色校准导致的重大视频损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-169">Fixes major video corruption with Color calibration.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-170">解决了 "电源" 菜单中的文本可能被截断的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-170">Addresses an issue where text might be truncated in the Power menu.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-171">支持 RequirePrivateStoreOnly 策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-171">Enables support for the RequirePrivateStoreOnly policy.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-20h2--june-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-172">Windows版本20H2 –2021年6月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-172">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – June 2021 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-173">生成19041.1154</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-173">Build 19041.1154</span></span>

### <a name="added-support-for-some-telemetry-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-174">添加了对某些遥测策略的支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-174">Added support for some telemetry policies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-175">HoloLens 2 上现在支持以下遥测策略：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-175">The following telemetry policies are now supported on the HoloLens 2:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-176">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-176">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-178">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-178">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-180">System\AllowTelemetry 和 System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx 都应该一起使用，以便对设置应用程序中的遥测和行为具有完全控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-180">Both System\AllowTelemetry and System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx should be used together to have complete control on the Telemetry and behavior in the Settings app.</span></span>

### <a name="introducing-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-264">新Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-264">Introducing the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

![将旧版徽标Microsoft Edge到新徽标Microsoft Edge动画](images/new-edge.gif)

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-266">新的Microsoft Edge[采用Chromium开放源代码](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2018/12/06/microsoft-edge-making-the-web-better-through-more-open-source-collaboration/)项目，为客户提供更好的兼容性，减少 Web 开发人员的 Web 碎片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-266">The new Microsoft Edge [adopts the Chromium open source project](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2018/12/06/microsoft-edge-making-the-web-better-through-more-open-source-collaboration/) to create better compatibility for customers and less fragmentation of the web for web developers.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-267">此Microsoft Edge会自动替换Microsoft Edge版本不再支持的旧版本。 [](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2021/03/09/microsoft-edge-legacy-end-of-support/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-267">This new Microsoft Edge automatically replaces legacy Microsoft Edge, which is [no longer supported](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2021/03/09/microsoft-edge-legacy-end-of-support/) in new releases.</span></span>

![新建Microsoft Edge屏幕截图](images/new-edge-ui.png)

#### <a name="launching-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-269">启动新Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-269">Launching the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-270">新的 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-270">The new Microsoft Edge</span></span> !["新建Microsoft Edge图标](images/new_edge_logo.png) <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-272"> (由蓝色和绿色 swirl 图标表示，) 图标固定到 "开始"菜单并且会在激活 Web 链接时自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-272">(represented by a blue and green swirl icon) is pinned to the Start menu and will automatically launch when you activate a web link.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-273">首次在 Microsoft Edge 启动HoloLens 2时，设置和数据会从旧版Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-273">When you first launch the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2, your settings and data will be imported from legacy Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-274">如果在启动新 Microsoft Edge后继续使用旧 Microsoft Edge，则新数据不会从旧 Microsoft Edge 同步到新Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-274">If you continue to use legacy Microsoft Edge after launching the new Microsoft Edge, that new data will not be synced from legacy Microsoft Edge to the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

#### <a name="configuring-policy-settings-for-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-275">配置新策略的策略Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-275">Configuring policy settings for the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-276">新Microsoft Edge为 IT 管理员提供了一组范围更广的浏览器策略，HoloLens 2旧策略中以前提供的浏览器Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-276">The new Microsoft Edge offers IT admins a much broader set of browser policies on HoloLens 2 than were previously available with legacy Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-277">下面是一些有用的资源，用于详细了解如何管理新应用的策略Microsoft Edge：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-277">Here are some helpful resources for learning more about managing policy settings for the new Microsoft Edge:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-278">使用 Microsoft Edge 配置策略Microsoft Intune</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-278">Configure Microsoft Edge policy settings with Microsoft Intune</span></span>](/deployedge/configure-edge-with-intune)
- [<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-279">Microsoft Edge 旧版Microsoft Edge映射</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-279">Microsoft Edge Legacy to Microsoft Edge policy mapping</span></span>](/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge)
- [<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-280">Google Chrome 到 Microsoft Edge策略映射</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-280">Google Chrome to Microsoft Edge policy mapping</span></span>](/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-chrome-to-newedge)
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-281">完整[Microsoft Edge Enterprise文档](/deployedge/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-281">Full [Microsoft Edge Enterprise documentation](/deployedge/)</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-282">由于新策略支持的浏览器策略Microsoft Edge，我们的团队无法保证每个新策略都适用于HoloLens 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-282">Because of the volume of browser policies supported by the new Microsoft Edge, our team is unable to guarantee that each new policy works on HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-283">但是，我们测试并确认新策略Microsoft Edge每个旧 Microsoft Edge策略的等效项，HoloLens 2正常工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-283">However, we've tested and confirmed than the new Microsoft Edge equivalent of each legacy Microsoft Edge policy previously supported on HoloLens 2 work as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-284">请参阅[Microsoft Edge 旧版Microsoft Edge映射](/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge)，查找与Microsoft Edge浏览器策略Microsoft Edge旧版浏览器策略等效的新HoloLens 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-284">See [Microsoft Edge Legacy to Microsoft Edge policy mapping](/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge) to find the new Microsoft Edge equivalent of each legacy Microsoft Edge browser policy you were using with HoloLens 2.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-285">我们知道至少有两个新的Microsoft Edge策略 *将不能* 与HoloLens 2：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-285">There are at least two new Microsoft Edge policies that we know *will not* work with HoloLens 2:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-286">EnterpriseModeSiteList</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-286">EnterpriseModeSiteList</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-287">EnterpriseSiteListServiceURL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-287">EnterpriseSiteListServiceURL</span></span>

#### <a name="what-to-expect-from-the-new-microsoft-edge-on-hololens-2"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-288">在 HoloLens 2 上新Microsoft Edge预期HoloLens 2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-288">What to expect from the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-289">由于新Microsoft Edge是本机 Win32 应用，具有新的 UWP 适配器层，允许它在 HoloLens 2 等仅 UWP 设备上运行，因此某些功能可能不会立即可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-289">Because the new Microsoft Edge is a native Win32 app with a new UWP adapter layer allowing it to run on UWP-only devices like HoloLens 2, some features may not be immediately available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-290">我们将支持未来几个月的新方案和功能，因此请查看此空间了解最新信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-290">We'll be supporting new scenarios and features over the coming months, so check this space for up-to-date information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-291">**方案和功能预期可正常工作：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-291">**Scenarios and features expected to work:**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-292">首次运行体验、登录到配置文件和同步</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-292">First-run experience, sign in to profile, and sync</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-293">网站应按预期呈现和行为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-293">Websites should render and behave as expected</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-294">大多数浏览器功能 (收藏夹、历史记录等) 应正常工作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-294">Most browser functionality (Favorites, History, etc.) should work as expected</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-295">深色模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-295">Dark mode</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-296">将 Web 应用安装到设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-296">Installing web apps to the device</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-297">安装扩展 (请使用任何无法正常使用扩展的扩展，请HoloLens 2) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-297">Installing extensions (please let us know if you use any extensions that don't work properly on HoloLens 2)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-298">查看和标记 PDF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-298">Viewing and marking up a PDF</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-299">单个浏览器窗口中的空间声音</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-299">Spatial sound from a single browser window</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-300">自动和手动更新浏览器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-300">Automatic and manual updating of the browser</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-301">使用 "保存到 PDF" 选项从 "打印" 菜单保存 PDF () </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-301">Saving a PDF from the Print menu (using "Save to PDF" option)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-302">WebXR 和360查看器扩展</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-302">WebXR and 360 Viewer extension</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-303">当跨环境中的多个窗口进行浏览时，内容还原到正确的窗口</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-303">Content restoration to correct window, when browsing across multiple windows placed in your environment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-304">**不应工作的方案和功能：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-304">**Scenarios and features not expected to work:**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-305">带有同时音频流的多个窗口的空间音效</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-305">Spatial sound from multiple windows with simultaneous audio streams</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-306">"看，说它"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-306">"See it, say it"</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-307">打印</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-307">Printing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-308">**最常见的浏览器已知问题：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-308">**Top browser known issues:**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-309">为新的 Microsoft Edge 禁用了全息键盘中的放大镜预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-309">The magnifier preview in the holographic keyboard has been disabled for the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-310">我们希望在未来的更新中重新启用此功能，一旦放大倍数工作正常。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-310">We hope to reenable this feature in a future update, once the magnification is working correctly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-311">如果有另一个浏览器窗口处于打开和活动状态，则可以从错误的浏览器窗口播放音频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-311">Audio may play from the wrong browser window if you have another browser window open and active.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-312">通过关闭不应播放音频的其他活动窗口，可以解决此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-312">You can work around this issue by closing the other active window that isn't supposed to be playing audio.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-313">在 ["关注我" 模式下](hololens2-basic-usage.md#follow-me-stop-following)从浏览器窗口播放音频时，如果禁用 "关注我" 模式，则音频将继续播放。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-313">When playing audio from a browser window in ["Follow me" mode](hololens2-basic-usage.md#follow-me-stop-following), the audio will continue playing if you disable "Follow me" mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-314">可以通过在禁用 "关注我" 模式之前停止音频播放，或通过使用 **X** 按钮关闭窗口，来解决此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-314">You can work around this issue by stopping audio playback before disabling "Follow me" mode or by closing the window with the **X** button.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-315">与 active Microsoft Edge windows 交互可能会导致其他2d 应用程序窗口意外停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-315">Interacting with active Microsoft Edge windows may cause other 2D app windows to go inactive unexpectedly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-316">您可以重新激活这些窗口，方法是再次与它们进行交互。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-316">You can reactivate these windows by interacting with them again.</span></span>

#### <a name="microsoft-edge-insider-channels"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-317">Microsoft Edge内部渠道</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-317">Microsoft Edge Insider channels</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-318">Microsoft Edge 团队使三个预览频道可供边缘有问必答社区使用： Beta 版、开发人员和未之用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-318">The Microsoft Edge team makes three preview channels available to the Edge Insider community: Beta, Dev, and Canary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-319">安装预览频道不会卸载 HoloLens 2 上的 Microsoft Edge 的发行版，并且可以同时安装多个版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-319">Installing a preview channel doesn't uninstall the released version of Microsoft Edge on your HoloLens 2, and you can install more than one at the same time.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-320">请访问[Microsoft Edge 有问必答主页](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com)以了解有关边缘有问必答社区的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-320">Visit the [Microsoft Edge Insider homepage](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com) to learn more about the Edge Insider community.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-321">若要详细了解不同的边缘有问必答通道并开始，请访问 [边缘有问必答下载页面](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-321">To learn more about the different Edge Insider channels and get started, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-322">有几种方法可用于安装 Microsoft Edge 有问必答通道 HoloLens 2：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-322">There are a couple methods available for installing Microsoft Edge Insider channels to HoloLens 2:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-323">**直接安装在设备上 (当前仅适用于非托管设备)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-323">**Direct install on device (currently only available to unmanaged devices)**</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-324">在 HoloLens 2 上，请访问[边缘有问必答下载页面](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-324">On your HoloLens 2, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-325">选择要安装的边缘有问必答频道的 "**下载 HoloLens 2** " 按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-325">Select the **Download for HoloLens 2** button for the Edge Insider channel you wish to install.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-326">使用文件资源管理器) ，从边缘下载队列或设备的 "下载" 文件夹启动下载的 .msix 文件 (。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-326">Launch the downloaded .msix file from the Edge download queue or from your device's "Downloads" folder (using File Explorer).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-327">将启动[应用安装程序](app-deploy-app-installer.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-327">[App installer](app-deploy-app-installer.md) will launch.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-328">选择“安装”按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-328">Select the **Install** button.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-329">安装成功后，会在 "开始"菜单的 "**所有应用**" 列表中找到 Microsoft Edge Beta、开发或工作方式为单独的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-329">After successful install, you'll find Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev, or Canary as a separate entry in the **All apps** list of the Start menu.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-330">**通过电脑安装 Windows 设备门户 (需要在 HoloLens 2 启用 [开发人员模式](/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#setting-up-hololens-to-use-windows-device-portal))**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-330">**Install via PC with Windows Device Portal (requires [developer mode](/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#setting-up-hololens-to-use-windows-device-portal) to be enabled on HoloLens 2)**</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-331">在你的电脑上，访问 [边缘有问必答下载页面](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-331">On your PC, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-332">选择要安装的边缘有问必答频道的 "下载 Windows 10" 按钮旁的 **下拉箭头按钮**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-332">Select the **drop-down arrow button** next to the "Download for Windows 10" button for the Edge Insider channel you wish to install.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-333">在下拉菜单中选择 " **HoloLens 2** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-333">Select **HoloLens 2** in the drop-down menu.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-334">将 .msix 文件保存到你的电脑的 "下载" 文件夹中 (或可轻松找到) 的其他文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-334">Save the .msix file to the "Downloads" folder of your PC (or another folder you can easily find).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-335">使用电脑上[Windows 设备门户](/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#installing-an-app)在 HoloLens 2 上安装下载的 .msix 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-335">Use [Windows Device Portal](/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#installing-an-app) on your PC to install the downloaded .msix file on HoloLens 2.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-336">安装成功后，会在 "开始"菜单的 "**所有应用**" 列表中找到 Microsoft Edge Beta、开发或工作方式为单独的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-336">After successful install, you'll find Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev, or Canary as a separate entry in the **All apps** list of the Start menu.</span></span>

#### <a name="using-wdac-to-block-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-337">使用 WDAC 阻止新 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-337">Using WDAC to block new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-338">对于希望更新其[WDAC 策略](windows-defender-application-control-wdac.md)以阻止新的 Microsoft Edge 应用的 IT 管理员，需要将以下项添加到策略中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-338">For IT Admins looking to update their [WDAC policy](windows-defender-application-control-wdac.md) to block the new Microsoft Edge app, you'll need to add the following to your policy.</span></span>

``` <Deny ID="ID_DENY_D_3_0" FriendlyName="C:\Data\Programs FileRule" PackageVersion="65535.65535.65535.65535" FileName="msedge.exe" /> ```

#### <a name="managing-endpoints-for-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-339">管理新 Microsoft Edge 的终结点</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-339">Managing endpoints for the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-340">出于考虑，某些环境可能具有网络限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-340">Some environments may have network restrictions to account for as a consideration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-341">若要确保具有新边缘的流畅体验，请 [启用这些 Microsoft 终结点。](/deployedge/microsoft-edge-security-endpoints)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-341">To ensure a smooth experience with the new Edge please [enable these Microsoft endpoints.](/deployedge/microsoft-edge-security-endpoints)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-342">阅读有关 HoloLens 当前可用[终结点](hololens-offline.md)的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-342">Read more about the currently available [endpoints for HoloLens](hololens-offline.md).</span></span>

### <a name="install-web-apps"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-343">安装 web 应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-343">Install web apps</span></span>
 > [!Note]
><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-344">从[Windows 全息版本 21H1](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-21h1)，Office web 应用将不再预装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-344">As of [Windows Holographic, version 21H1](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-21h1), the Office web app will no longer be pre-installed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-345">你可以使用新边缘来安装 web 应用和 Microsoft Store 应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-345">You can use the new Edge to install web apps alongside Microsoft Store apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-346">例如，可以安装 Microsoft Office web 应用来查看和编辑托管在 SharePoint 或 OneDrive 上的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-346">For example, you can install the Microsoft Office web app to view and edit files hosted on SharePoint or OneDrive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-347">若要安装 Office web 应用，请访问， https://www.office.com 并在地址栏中选择 "**可用应用**" 或 "**安装 Office** " 按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-347">To install the Office web app, visit https://www.office.com and select the **App Available** or **Install Office** button in the address bar.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-348">选择 " **安装** " 进行确认。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-348">Select **Install** to confirm.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-349">仅当 HoloLens 2 具有活动的 internet 连接时，Office web 应用功能才可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-349">Office web app functionality is only available when your HoloLens 2 has an active internet connection.</span></span>

### <a name="webxr-and-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-350">WebXR 和360查看器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-350">WebXR and 360 Viewer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-351">新 Microsoft Edge 包括对 WebXR 的支持，这是用于创建沉浸式 web 体验 (替换 WebVR) 的新标准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-351">The new Microsoft Edge includes support for WebXR, which is the new standard for creating immersive web experiences (replacing WebVR).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-352">许多沉浸式 web 体验在设计上都是使用 VR (它们将视图的字段替换为虚拟环境) ，但 HoloLens 2 也支持这些体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-352">Many immersive web experiences were designed with VR in mind (they replace your field of view with a virtual environment), but these experiences are also supported by HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-353">WebXR 标准还启用了使用物理环境的扩充和混合现实沉浸式 web 体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-353">The WebXR standard also enables augmented and mixed reality immersive web experiences that use your physical environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-354">随着开发人员花更多时间来 WebXR，我们预计新增加和混合现实沉浸式体验将会让 HoloLens 2 客户尝试！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-354">As developers spend more time with WebXR, we anticipate new augmented and mixed reality immersive experiences will arrive for HoloLens 2 customers to try!</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-355">360查看器扩展是在 WebXR 上构建的，并随新 Microsoft Edge 在 HoloLens 2 上自动安装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-355">The 360 Viewer extension is built on WebXR and automatically installs alongside the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-356">此 web 扩展使你能够在360度视频中从而深入了解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-356">This web extension gives you the ability to immerse yourself in 360-degree videos.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-357">YouTube 提供最大程度的360视频，因此我们鼓励你从这里开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-357">YouTube offers the largest selection of 360 videos, so we encourage you to start there.</span></span>

#### <a name="how-to-use-webxr"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-358">如何使用 WebXR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-358">How to use WebXR</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-359">导航到支持 WebXR 的网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-359">Navigate to a website with WebXR support.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-360">选择网站上的 " **输入** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-360">Select the **Enter VR** button on the website.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-361">此按钮的位置和视觉表示形式可能因网站而异，但它看起来可能类似于：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-361">The location and visual representation of this button may vary per website, but it may look similar to:</span></span>

    ![输入 VR 按钮示例](images/75px-enter-vr.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-363">首次尝试在特定域上启动 WebXR 体验时，浏览器将要求同意输入沉浸式视图，并选择 " **允许**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-363">The first time you try to launch a WebXR experience on a specific domain, the browser will ask for consent to enter an immersive view, select **Allow**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-364">使用[HoloLens 2 手势](hololens2-basic-usage.md#the-hand-tracking-frame)来处理体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-364">Use [HoloLens 2 gestures](hololens2-basic-usage.md#the-hand-tracking-frame) to manipulate the experience.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-365">如果体验没有 **退出** 按钮，请使用 [开始手势](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) 返回 home。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-365">If the experience doesn't have an **Exit** button, use the [Start gesture](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) to return home.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-366">**建议的 WebXR 示例**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-366">**Recommended WebXR samples**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-367">360查看器 (参阅下一节) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-367">360 Viewer (see next section)</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-368">XR 恐龙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-368">XR Dinosaurs</span></span>](https://www.xrdinosaurs.com/)
- [<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-369">Barista Express</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-369">Barista Express</span></span>](https://constructarca.de/game/barista-express/)
- [<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-370">WebXR 画图</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-370">WebXR Paint</span></span>](https://threejs.org/examples/webxr_vr_paint.html)

#### <a name="how-to-use-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-371">如何使用360查看器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-371">How to use 360 Viewer</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-372">在 YouTube 上导航到360度视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-372">Navigate to a 360-degree video on YouTube.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-373">在视频帧中，选择混合现实耳机按钮：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-373">In the video frame, select the mixed reality headset button:</span></span>

    ![用于激活360查看器的按钮](images/enter-360-viewer.jpg)

1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-375">首次尝试在特定域上启动360查看器时，浏览器将要求同意输入沉浸式视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-375">The first time you try to launch 360 Viewer on a specific domain, the browser will ask for consent to enter an immersive view.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-376">选择“允许”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-376">Select **Allow**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-377">[点击](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) 以打开播放控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-377">[Air tap](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) to bring up the playback controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-378">使用 " [手" 光线和 "空中点击](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) " 播放/暂停、向前/向后、打开/关闭字幕或停止体验 (会退出沉浸式视图) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-378">Use [hand rays and air tap](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) to play/pause, skip forward/back, turn captions on/off, or stop the experience (which exits the immersive view).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-379">播放控件将在几秒钟处于非活动状态后消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-379">The playback controls will disappear after a few seconds of inactivity.</span></span>

#### <a name="top-webxr-and-360-viewer-known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-380">最 WebXR 和360查看器已知问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-380">Top WebXR and 360 Viewer known issues</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-381">根据 WebXR 体验的复杂性，帧速率可能下降或断断续续。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-381">Depending on the complexity of the WebXR experience, the framerate may drop or stutter.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-382">默认情况下，不支持 WebXR 中的已表述的手接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-382">Support for articulated hand joints in WebXR is not enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-383">开发人员可以 `edge://flags` 通过打开 "WebXR 手型输入" 启用支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-383">Developers can enable support via `edge://flags` by turning on "WebXR Hand Input."</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-384">360之外的网站中的视频不会按预期方式工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-384">360 videos from websites other than YouTube may not work as expected.</span></span>

#### <a name="providing-feedback-on-webxr-and-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-385">在 WebXR 和360查看器中提供反馈</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-385">Providing feedback on WebXR and 360 Viewer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-386">请通过新 Microsoft Edge 中的 "**发送反馈**" 功能与我们的团队共享反馈和 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-386">Please share feedback and bugs with our team via the **Send Feedback** feature in the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

### <a name="new-settings-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-387">新建设置应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-387">New Settings app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-388">在此版本中，我们引入了新版本的设置应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-388">With this release, we're introducing a new version of the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-389">新的设置应用程序包括以下方面 HoloLens 2 的新功能和扩展的设置：声音、电源 & 睡眠、网络 & Internet、应用、帐户、轻松访问等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-389">The new Settings app includes new features and expanded settings for HoloLens 2 in the following areas: Sound, Power & sleep, Network & Internet, Apps, Accounts, Ease of Access, and more.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-390">由于新的设置应用与旧设置应用不同，因此在更新时将删除以前在环境中放置的任何设置窗口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-390">Because the new Settings app is distinct from the legacy Settings app, any Settings windows you previously placed around your environment will be removed upon update.</span></span>

![新设置应用主页](images/new-settings-app.png)

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-392">**新功能和设置**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-392">**New features and settings**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-393">设置搜索：使用关键字或设置的名称从设置主页搜索设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-393">Settings search: search for settings from the Settings homepage using keywords or the setting's name.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-394">系统 > 声音：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-394">System > Sound:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-395">输入和输出音频设备：例如，单独选择输入和输出音频设备 (例如，通过蓝牙耳机收听音频，或使用 USB C 麦克风进行音频输入) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-395">Input and output audio devices: independently choose your input and output audio devices (for example, listen to audio via Bluetooth headphones or use a USB-C microphone for audio input).</span></span>
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-396">HoloLens 2 不支持蓝牙麦克风。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-396">Bluetooth microphones are not supported by HoloLens 2.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-397">应用卷：独立调整每个应用的音量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-397">App volume: independently adjust the volume of each app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-398">请参阅 [每个应用音量控制](#per-app-volume-control)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-398">See [per app volume control](#per-app-volume-control).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-399">系统 > Power & 睡眠：在设备处于非活动状态一段时间后，选择设备应进入睡眠状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-399">System > Power & sleep: choose when the device should go to sleep after a period of inactivity.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-400">系统 > 电池：手动启用节电模式，或设置节电模式自动开启的电池阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-400">System > Battery: manually enable battery saver mode or set a battery threshold at which point battery saver mode turns on automatically.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-401">设备> USB：默认情况下可以禁用 USB 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-401">Devices > USB: you can disable USB connections by default.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-402">网络& Internet：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-402">Network & Internet:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-403">USB-C 以太网适配器现在会显示在 Internet &中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-403">USB-C Ethernet adapters will now appear in Network & Internet.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-404">USB-C 以太网适配器设置现已可用，包括其 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-404">USB-C Ethernet adapter settings are now available, including its IP address.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-405">现在可以在飞机上启用飞行HoloLens 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-405">You can now enable airplane mode on HoloLens 2.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-406">应用：可以重置用于文件和链接类型的默认应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-406">Apps: you can reset the default apps used for file and link types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-407">有关详细信息，请参阅 [默认应用选取器](#default-app-picker)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-407">For more information see [Default app picker](#default-app-picker).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-408">帐户>其他用户：设备所有者可以添加用户、将标准用户升级到设备所有者、将设备所有者降级为标准用户以及删除用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-408">Accounts > Other users: device owners can add users, upgrade standard users to device owners, downgrade device owners to standard users, and remove users.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-409">易于访问：更改文本大小和一些视觉效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-409">Ease of Access: change text size and some visual effects.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-410">**已知问题**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-410">**Known issues**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-411">将删除设置放置的窗口 (请参阅上面的) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-411">Previously placed Settings windows will be removed (see note above).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-412">无法再使用应用重命名设备设置应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-412">You can no longer rename your device with the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-413">IT 管理员可以 Windows使用适用于 HoloLens 2 设备名称模板或 MDM [DevDetail CSP](/windows/client-management/mdm/devdetail-csp) Ext/Microsoft/DNSComputerName 节点的[Autopilot](hololens2-autopilot.md)来重命名设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-413">IT admins can rename devices by using the [Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2](hololens2-autopilot.md) device name template or the MDM [DevDetail CSP](/windows/client-management/mdm/devdetail-csp) Ext/Microsoft/DNSComputerName node.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-414">"以太网"页显示一个 ("UsbNcm") 虚拟以太网设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-414">The Ethernet page shows a virtual Ethernet device ("UsbNcm") at all times.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-415">新应用程序的电池Microsoft Edge可能不准确，因为 UWP 适配器层支持 Win32 桌面应用程序，因此 (即将修复) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-415">Battery usage for the new Microsoft Edge may not be accurate, due to its nature as a Win32 desktop application supported by a UWP adapter layer (no fix anticipated soon).</span></span>

#### <a name="display-color-calibration"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-416">显示颜色校准</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-416">Display color calibration</span></span>



<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-417">借助此新设置，可以选择其他颜色配置文件来显示HoloLens 2配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-417">With this new setting, you can select an alternative color profile for your HoloLens 2 display.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-418">这有助于颜色看起来更准确，尤其是在较低的显示亮度级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-418">This may help colors appear more accurate, especially at lower display brightness levels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-419">可以在"系统校准"页上的设置应用中找到显示>校准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-419">Display color calibration can be found in the Settings app, on the System > Calibration page.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-420">由于此设置将新的颜色配置文件保存到显示固件，因此它是每个设备设置 (，并非每个用户帐户) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-420">Because this setting saves a new color profile to your display firmware, it is a per-device setting (and not unique to each user account).</span></span>

##### <a name="how-to-use-display-color-calibration"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-421">如何使用显示颜色校准</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-421">How to use display color calibration</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-422">启动 **设置** 应用并导航到 **"系统>校准"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-422">Launch the **Settings** app and navigate to **System > Calibration**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-423">在 **"显示颜色校准"** 下，选择 **"运行显示颜色校准"** 按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-423">Under **Display color calibration**, select the **Run display color calibration** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-424">显示颜色校准体验将启动，鼓励你确保视器处于正确的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-424">The display color calibration experience will launch and encourage you to make sure your visor is in the correct position.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-425">在继续浏览指令对话框后，显示将自动灰显为 30% 的亮度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-425">After you proceed through the instruction dialog boxes, your display will automatically be dimmed to 30% brightness.</span></span>
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-426">如果在环境中看到灰色场景时遇到问题，可以使用设备左侧的亮度按钮手动HoloLens 2亮度级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-426">If you're having trouble seeing the dimmed scene in your environment, you can manually adjust the brightness level of HoloLens 2 using the brightness buttons on the left side of the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-427">选择按钮 1-6 可立即试用每个颜色配置文件，并找到最适合你眼睛的颜色配置文件 (这通常意味着有助于场景显示最中性、灰度模式和外观色调按预期呈现的配置文件。) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-427">Select buttons 1-6 to instantly try out each color profile, and find one that looks the best to your eyes (this usually means the profile that helps the scene appear most neutral, with the grayscale pattern and skin tones looking as expected.)</span></span>

    ![显示颜色校准场景](images/color-cal-ui.png)
    
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-429">如果对所选配置文件满意，请选择"保存& **退出"** 按钮</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-429">When you're happy with the selected profile, select the **Save & Exit** button</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-430">如果不想进行更改，请选择"取消& **退出"** 按钮，所做的更改将还原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-430">If you prefer not to make changes, select the **Cancel & Exit** button and your changes will be reverted</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-431">下面是使用显示颜色校准设置时请记住的一些有用提示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-431">Here are some helpful tips to keep in mind while using the display color calibration setting:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-432">可以随时从设置重新运行显示颜色校准</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-432">You can re-run display color calibration from Settings whenever you'd like</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-433">如果设备上有人以前使用过此设置来更改颜色配置文件，则最近更改的日期/时间将反映在设置页面上</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-433">If anyone on the device has previously used the setting to change color profiles, the date/time of the most recent change will be reflected on the Settings page</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-434">重新运行显示颜色校准时，将突出显示以前保存的颜色配置文件，并且"配置文件 0"将不会 (因为"配置文件 0"表示显示的原始颜色配置文件) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-434">When you re-run display color calibration, the color profile that was previously saved will be highlighted and Profile 0 will not appear (as Profile 0 represents the display's original color profile)</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-435">如果要还原到显示的原始颜色配置文件，可以从"颜色"页设置还原[ (了解如何重置](#how-to-reset-color-profile)颜色配置文件) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-435">If you want to revert to the display's original color profile, you can do so from the Settings page (see [how to reset color profile](#how-to-reset-color-profile))</span></span>

##### <a name="how-to-reset-color-profile"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-436">如何重置颜色配置文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-436">How to reset color profile</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-437">如果对保存到自定义颜色配置文件HoloLens 2，可以还原设备的原始颜色配置文件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-437">If you're unhappy with the custom color profile saved to your HoloLens 2, you can restore the device's original color profile:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-438">启动 **设置** 应用并导航到 **"系统>校准"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-438">Launch the **Settings** app and navigate to **System > Calibration**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-439">在 **"显示颜色校准"** 下，选择" **重置为默认颜色配置文件"** 按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-439">Under **Display color calibration**, select the **Reset to default color profile** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-440">当对话框打开时 **，如果已准备好** 重启应用并应用HoloLens 2，请选择"重启"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-440">When the dialog box opens, select **Restart** if you're ready to restart HoloLens 2 and apply your changes.</span></span>

#### <a name="top-display-color-calibration-known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-441">顶部显示颜色校准已知问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-441">Top display color calibration known issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-442">在设置页上，指示上次更改颜色配置文件时间的状态字符串将过期，直到重新加载该页设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-442">On the Settings page, the status string that tells you when the color profile was last changed will be out of date until you reload that page of Settings.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-443">解决方法：选择另设置页，然后重新选择"校准"页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-443">Workaround: Select another Settings page and then re-select the Calibration page.</span></span>

#### <a name="default-app-picker"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-444">默认应用选取器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-444">Default app picker</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-445">激活超链接或打开具有多个已安装应用（支持它）的文件类型时，将看到一个新窗口打开，提示你选择哪个已安装的应用应处理文件或链接类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-445">When you activate a hyperlink or open a file type with more than one installed app, which supports it, you will see a new window open prompting you to select which installed app should handle the file or link type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-446">在此窗口中，还可以选择让所选应用处理文件或链接类型"一次"或"始终"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-446">In this window, you can also choose to have the selected app handle the file or link type "Once" or "Always."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-447">如果选择"始终"，但以后想要更改处理特定文件或链接类型的应用，可以在"应用"中重置设置 >**默认值**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-447">If you choose "Always" but later want to change which app handles a particular file or link type, you can reset your saved defaults in **Settings > Apps**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-448">滚动到页面底部，选择"文件类型的默认应用"和/或"链接类型的默认应用"下的"清除"按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-448">Scroll to the bottom of the page and select the **Clear** button under "Default apps for file types" and/or "Default apps for link types."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-449">与台式电脑上的类似设置不同，无法重置单个文件类型默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-449">Unlike the similar setting on desktop PCs, you can't reset individual file type defaults.</span></span>

#### <a name="per-app-volume-control"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-450">每个应用音量控制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-450">Per app volume control</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-451">现在在此Windows中，用户可以手动调整每个应用的卷级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-451">Now in this Windows build, users can manually adjust the volume level of each app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-452">这样，用户可以更好地专注于所需的应用，或在使用多个应用时更好地听到这些应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-452">This allows for users to better focus on the apps that they need to, or better hear when using multiple apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-453">例如，需要关闭一个应用的数量，同时调用另一个人在另一个应用中进行远程协助。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-453">Such as needing to turn down volume of one app while calling another person for remote assistance in another.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-454">若要设置单个应用的音量，请导航到"设置声音"，并在"**高级** 声音选项"下  ->    ->  选择"应用 **音量和设备首选项"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-454">To set the volume of an individual app navigate to **Settings** -> **System** -> **Sound**, and under Advanced sound options select **App volume and device preferences**.</span></span><br/><br/>

<img alt="App volume and device preferences." src="./images/volume-per-app.jpg" width="500" height="250" />

#### <a name="swipe-to-type"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-455">轻扫以键入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-455">Swipe to type</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-456">一些客户发现，通过轻扫要键入的单词的形状，在虚拟键盘上"键入"速度更快，我们正在预览全息键盘的此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-456">Some customers find it faster to "type" on virtual keyboards by swiping the shape of the word they intend to type, and we're previewing this feature for the holographic keyboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-457">可以通过将手指的尖通过全息键盘的平面，轻扫该单词的形状，然后从键盘平面中收回手指的提示，一次轻扫一个词。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-457">You can swipe one word at a time by passing the tip of your finger through the plane of the holographic keyboard, swiping the shape of the word, and then withdrawing the tip of your finger from the plane of the keyboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-458">通过从键盘上删除单词之间的手指，无需按空格键即可轻扫后续字词。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-458">You can swipe follow up words without needing to press the space bar by removing your finger from the keyboard between words.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-459">如果在键盘上手指移动后看到轻扫线索，则你会知道该功能正在工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-459">You will know the feature is working if you see a swipe trail following your finger's movement on the keyboard.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-460">请注意，此功能可能难以使用和掌握，因为全息键盘的性质与手机显示设备不同， (对手指的抵御) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-460">Please note, this feature can be tricky to use and master because of the nature of a holographic keyboard where you don't feel resistance against your finger (unlike a mobile phone display).</span></span> 

### <a name="power-menu-from-start"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-461">"开始"中的电源菜单</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-461">Power menu from Start</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-462">允许用户注销、关闭和重启设备的新菜单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-462">A new menu that allows the user to sign out, shut down and restart the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-463">显示系统HoloLens “开始”屏幕可用时间的指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-463">An indicator in the HoloLens Start screen that shows when a system update is available.</span></span>

### <a name="multiple-users-listed-on-sign-in-screen"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-474">登录屏幕上列出的多个用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-474">Multiple users listed on Sign in screen</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-475">以前，"登录"屏幕只显示最近登录的用户，以及"其他用户"入口点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-475">Previously the Sign In screen showed only the most recently signed in user, as well as an 'Other user' entry point.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-476">我们已收到客户反馈，如果多个用户已登录到设备，这是不够的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-476">We have received customer feedback that this not sufficient if multiple users have signed into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-477">他们仍然需要重新键入其用户名等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-477">They were still required to retype their username etc.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-478">本Windows中引入，在选择"PIN输入"字段右侧"其他用户"时，"登录"屏幕将显示以前已登录到设备的多个用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-478">Introduced in this Windows build, when selecting **Other user** which is located to the right of the PIN entry field, the Sign in screen will display multiple users with have previously signed into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-479">这允许用户选择其用户配置文件，然后使用其凭据Windows Hello登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-479">This allows users to select their user profile and then sign-in using their Windows Hello credentials.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-480">还可通过"添加帐户"按钮从此"其他用户"页将新 **用户添加到** 设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-480">A new user can also be added to the device from this Other users page via the **Add account** button.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-481">在"其他用户"菜单中，"其他用户"按钮将显示最后一个登录到设备的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-481">When in the Other users menu, the Other users button will display the last user signed into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-482">选择此按钮可返回到此用户的"登录"屏幕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-482">Select this button to return to the Sign in screen for this user.</span></span>

### <a name="usb-c-external-microphone-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-485">USB-C 外部麦克风支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-485">USB-C External Microphone Support</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-486">插入 **USB 麦克风不会自动将其设置为输入设备**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-486">Plugging in **a USB mic will not automatically set it as the input device**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-487">在插入一组 USB-C 耳机时，用户将观察到耳机的音频将自动重定向到耳机，但 HoloLens OS 会将内部麦克风阵列的优先级设置为高于任何其他输入设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-487">When plugging in a set of USB-C headphones users will observe that the headphone's audio will automatically be redirected to the headphones, but the HoloLens OS prioritizes the internal microphone array above any other input device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-488">**若要使用 USB-C 麦克风，请执行以下步骤。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-488">**In order to use a USB-C microphone follow the steps below.**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-489">用户可以使用"声音设置"面板选择已连接 USB-C **的外部** 麦克风。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-489">Users can select USB-C connected external microphones using the **Sound** settings panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-490">USB-C 麦克风可用于通话、录制等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-490">USB-C microphones can be used for calling, recording, etc.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-491">打开 **"设置"** 应用，然后选择"**系统**  >  **声音"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-491">Open the **Settings** app and select **System** > **Sound**.</span></span>

![声音设置](images/usbc-mic-1.jpg)

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-493">若要将外部麦克风与 **Remote Assist，用户** 需要单击"管理声音设备"超链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-493">To use external microphones with **Remote Assist**, users will need to click the “Manage sound devices” hyperlink.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-494">然后，使用下拉列表将外部麦克风设置为"默认" **或** " **通信默认值"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-494">Then use the drop-down to set the external microphone as either **Default** or **Communications Default.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-495">选择 **"** 默认"意味着外部麦克风将在所有位置使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-495">Choosing **Default** means that the external microphone will be used everywhere.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-496">选择 **"** 通信默认值"意味着外部麦克风将用于 Remote Assist和其他通信应用，但HoloLens麦克风阵列仍可用于其他任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-496">Choosing **Communications Default** means that the external microphone will be used in Remote Assist and other communications apps, but the HoloLens mic array may still be used for other tasks.</span></span>

#### <a name="what-about-bluetooth-microphone-support&quot;></a><span data-ttu-id=&quot;cbae1-499&quot;>麦克风支持蓝牙呢？</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;cbae1-499&quot;>What about Bluetooth microphone support?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id=&quot;cbae1-500&quot;>遗憾的是，蓝牙当前仍不支持麦克风HoloLens 2。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;cbae1-500&quot;>Unfortunately Bluetooth microphones are still not currently supported on HoloLens 2.</span></span>

#### <a name=&quot;troubleshooting-usb-c-microphones&quot;></a><span data-ttu-id=&quot;cbae1-501&quot;>USB-C 麦克风疑难解答</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;cbae1-501&quot;>Troubleshooting USB-C microphones</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id=&quot;cbae1-502&quot;>请注意，某些 USB-C 麦克风会错误地将自身报告为麦克风 *和* 扬声器。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;cbae1-502&quot;>Be aware that some USB-C microphones incorrectly report themselves as both a microphone *and* a speaker.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id=&quot;cbae1-503&quot;>这是麦克风问题，而不是 HoloLens。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;cbae1-503&quot;>This is a problem with the microphone and not with HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id=&quot;cbae1-504&quot;>将其中一个麦克风插入 HoloLens 时，可能会丢失声音。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;cbae1-504&quot;>When plugging one of these microphones into HoloLens, sound may be lost.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id=&quot;cbae1-505&quot;>幸运的是，有一个简单的修补程序。</span><span class=&quot;sxs-lookup&quot;><span data-stu-id=&quot;cbae1-505&quot;>Fortunately there is a simple fix.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id=&quot;cbae1-506&quot;>在 **设置**  ->  **系统**  ->  **声音**&quot;中，将内置扬声器 **(模拟功能音频驱动程序")** 为 **默认设备**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-506">In **Settings** -> **System** -> **Sound**, explicitly set the built-in speakers **(Analog Feature Audio Driver)** as the **Default device**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-507">即使稍后会删除并重新连接麦克风，HoloLens 也应记住此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-507">HoloLens should remember this setting even if the microphone is removed and reconnected later.</span></span>

![USB-C 麦克风疑难解答](images/usbc-mic-4.png)

### <a name="visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-509">网亭的访问者自动登录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-509">Visitor Auto logon for Kiosks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-510">这项新功能使访问者帐户上的自动登录可用于展台模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-510">This new feature enables the auto logon on Visitor accounts to be used for Kiosk modes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-511">对于非 AAD 配置，为访问者自动登录配置设备：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-511">For a non-AAD configuration, to configure a device for visitor auto-logon:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-512">创建一个预配包，其中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-512">Create a provisioning package that:</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-513">将 **运行时设置 AssignedAccess** 配置为允许访问者帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-513">Configures **Runtime settings/AssignedAccess** to allow Visitor accounts.</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-514">（可选）在 MDM **(运行时设置/工作区/注册)** 中注册设备，以便以后可以对其进行管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-514">Optionally enrolls the device in MDM **(Runtime settings/Workplace/Enrollments)** so that it can be managed later.</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-515">不创建本地帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-515">Do not create a local account</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-516">[应用设置包](hololens-provisioning.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-516">[Apply the provisioning package](hololens-provisioning.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-517">对于 AAD 配置，用户可以立即获得类似于此的内容，而无需进行此更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-517">For an AAD configuration, users can achieve something similar to this today without this change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-518">为展台模式配置的 AAD 加入设备可以通过在登录屏幕上点击一次按钮，登录访问者帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-518">AAD joined devices configured for kiosk mode can sign in a Visitor account with a single button tap from the sign in screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-519">登录到访问者帐户后，在从 "开始" 菜单中显式注销访问者或重新启动设备之前，该设备将不会提示登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-519">Once signed in to the visitor account, the device will not prompt for sign in again until the Visitor is explicitly signed out from the start menu or the device is restarted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-520">可以通过 [自定义 OMA URI](/mem/intune/configuration/custom-settings-windows-10) 策略来管理访问者自动登录：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-520">Visitor Auto logon can be managed via [custom OMA-URI](/mem/intune/configuration/custom-settings-windows-10) policy:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-521">URI 值：./Device/Vendor/MSFT/MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-521">URI value: ./Device/Vendor/MSFT/MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-522">策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-522">Policy</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-523">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-523">Description</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-524">配置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-524">Configurations</span></span>  |
|---|---|---|
