## <a name="windows-holographic-version-2004---september-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1058">Windows全息版，版本 2004-2020 更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1058">Windows Holographic, version 2004 - September 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1059">生成19041.1117</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1059">Build 19041.1117</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1060">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1060">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1061">解决了在 appxmanifest.xml 中存在 SupportsMultipleInstances = "true" 时阻止 Visual Studio 调试应用程序的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1061">Addresses an issue that prevented Visual Studio from debugging an application when SupportsMultipleInstances=”true” is present in the appxmanifest.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1062">此版本包含 NCSI proxy 检测修复，可解决通过网络代理进行的 Internet 检测失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1062">This release includes NCSI proxy detection fix to address failed Internet detection over network proxy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1063">NCSI 可以使用计算机代理和每个配置文件的代理来检测 Internet 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1063">NCSI can use machine proxy and per-profile proxy for Internet connectivity detection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1064">将来的版本中，NCSI 将支持每个用户的代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1064">Per-user proxy will be supported by NCSI in future release.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1065">在大多数 Windows Mixed Reality 设备上，当用户的头处于期待的非特定位置时，正向矢量平行于地面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1065">On most Windows Mixed Reality devices, the forward direction vector is parallel to the ground when the user's head is in a neutral position looking forward.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1066">但是，的较早版本 HoloLens 2 将矢量调整为垂直于显示面板，而相对于理想方向，该向量相对向下倾斜几度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1066">However, earlier versions of HoloLens 2 aligned the vector to be perpendicular to the display panels instead, which is tilted downward a few degrees relative to the ideal orientation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1067">HoloLens 2 的较新版本已更正此情况，以确保各种形式因素的语义一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1067">Newer versions of HoloLens 2 have corrected this to ensure semantic consistency across form factors.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1068">提高了手动跟踪可靠性，在特定情况下将导致更少的跟踪损失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1068">Improved hand tracking robustness that will result in fewer tracking losses in specific scenarios.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1069">此版本包含一个修补程序，可改进音频时间戳质量，这可能会导致视频捕获问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1069">This release contains a fix to improve audio timestamp quality which may have contributed to video capture issues.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---september-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1070">Windows全息版，版本 1903-2020 更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1070">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - September 2020 Update</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1109">修复了一个 bug，以提高混合现实捕获方案中的音频质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1109">Fixed a bug to improve audio quality in mixed reality capture scenarios.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1110">具体而言，此修复应消除在显示"开始"菜单时录制 **的音频** 问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1110">Specifically, this fix should eliminate audio glitching in the recording when the **Start** menu is displayed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1111">改进了录制视频中的全息影像稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1111">Improved hologram stability in recorded videos.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1112">解决了混合现实捕获在设备处于待机状态多天后无法录制视频的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1112">Resolved an issue where mixed reality capture couldn't record video after the device was left in standby state for multiple days.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1113">对于 Unity 应用程序，通常禁用 HolographicSpace.UserPresence API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1113">The HolographicSpace.UserPresence API is generally disabled for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1114">此行为可避免在视器翻转时导致某些应用暂停的问题，即使启用了"在后台运行"设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1114">This behavior avoids an issue that caused some apps to pause when the visor was flipped up, even if the "run in the background" setting was enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1115">现已为 Unity 版本 2018.4.18 及更高版本以及 2019.3.4 及更高版本启用 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1115">The API is now enabled for Unity versions 2018.4.18 and later and 2019.3.4 and later.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1116">通过证书设备门户访问Wi-Fi，Web 浏览器可能会由于证书无效而阻止对 的访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1116">When you access Device Portal over a Wi-Fi connection, a web browser might prevent access to due to an invalid certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1117">即使设备证书以前受信任，浏览器也可能报告"ERR_SSL_PROTOCOL_ERROR"等错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1117">The browser might report an error such as "ERR_SSL_PROTOCOL_ERROR," even if the device certificate was previously trusted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1118">在这种情况下，无法继续设备门户，因为无法忽略安全警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1118">In this case, you can't progress to Device Portal, as there's no option to ignore security warnings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1119">此更新解决了问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1119">This update resolved the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1120">如果以前在电脑上下载并信任设备证书以删除浏览器安全警告，并且发生 SSL 错误，必须下载并信任新证书，以解决浏览器安全警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1120">If the device certificate was previously downloaded and trusted on a PC to remove browser security warnings, and the SSL error occurs, the new certificate has to be downloaded and trusted to address browser security warnings.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1121">启用了创建运行时预配包的能力，该包可以使用 MSIX 包安装应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1121">Enabled the ability to create a runtime provisioning package that can install an app by using MSIX packages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1122">在 设置System 全息影像 中添加了一个设置，允许用户在设备关闭时自动从混合现实主页  >    >  中删除所有全息影像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1122">Added a setting in **Settings** > **System** > **Holograms** that allows users to automatically remove all holograms from Mixed Reality home when the device shuts down.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1123">修复了导致应用HoloLens像素格式在仿真器中呈现黑色HoloLens的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1123">Fixed an issue that caused HoloLens apps that change their pixel format to render black in the HoloLens emulator.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1124">修复了 Iris 登录期间导致崩溃的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1124">Fixed a bug that caused a crash during Iris login.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1125">修复了针对当前应用重复下载应用商店的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1125">Fixed an issue about repeated store downloads for already-current apps.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1126">修复了一个 bug，以防止沉浸式应用Microsoft Edge打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1126">Fixed a bug to prevent immersive apps from opening Microsoft Edge repeatedly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1127">修复了从 1903 版本更新后在初始启动中启动照片应用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1127">Fixed an issue with launches of the Photos app in initial boots after updating from the 1903 release.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1128">提高了性能和可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1128">Improved performance and reliability.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---june-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1129">Windows全息版 1903 - 2020 年 6 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1129">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - June 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1130">内部版本 18362.1064</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1130">Build 18362.1064</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1131">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1131">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1132">如果未指定某些属性，则自定义 MRC 记录器具有新的默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1132">Custom MRC recorders have new default values for certain properties if they aren't specified.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1133">在 *MRC 视频效果上*：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1133">On the *MRC Video Effect*:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1134">PreferredHologramPerspective (1 PhotoVideoCamera) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1134">PreferredHologramPerspective (1 PhotoVideoCamera)</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1135">GlobalOpacityCoefficient (0.9 (HoloLens) 1.0 (沉浸式头戴显示设备) ) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1135">GlobalOpacityCoefficient (0.9 (HoloLens) 1.0 (Immersive headset))</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1136">在 *MRC 音频效果上*：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1136">On the *MRC Audio Effect*:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1137">LoopbackGain (中"应用音频增益"页上的当前混合现实捕获"Windows 设备门户) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1137">LoopbackGain (the current "App Audio Gain" value on the Mixed Reality Capture page in Windows Device Portal)</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1138">MicrophoneGain (中"麦克风音频增益"页上的当前混合现实捕获"Windows 设备门户) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1138">MicrophoneGain (the current "Mic Audio Gain" value on the Mixed Reality Capture page in Windows Device Portal)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1139">对于 Unity 应用程序，通常禁用 HolographicSpace.UserPresence API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1139">The HolographicSpace.UserPresence API is generally disabled for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1140">此行为可避免在视器翻转时导致某些应用暂停的问题，即使启用了在后台运行的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1140">This behavior avoids an issue that causes some apps to pause when the visor is flipped up, even if the setting to run in the background is enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1141">现已为 Unity 版本 2018.4.18 及更高版本以及 2019.3.4 及更高版本启用 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1141">The API is now enabled for Unity versions 2018.4.18 and later, and 2019.3.4 and later.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1142">修复了导致应用HoloLens像素格式以在应用中呈现黑色HoloLens Emulator。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1142">Fixed an issue that caused HoloLens apps that change their pixel format to render black in the HoloLens Emulator.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1143">修复了从 1903 版本更新后在初始启动中启动照片应用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1143">Fixed an issue about launches of the Photos app in initial boots after updating from the 1903 release.</span></span>

### <a name="support-for-windows-autopilot"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1170">支持 Windows Autopilot</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1170">Support for Windows Autopilot</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1171">WindowsAutopilot for HoloLens 2允许设备销售渠道预先HoloLens Intune 租户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1171">Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 lets the device sales channel pre-enroll HoloLens into your Intune tenant.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1172">设备到达时，可以自行部署为租户下的共享设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1172">When devices arrive, they’re ready to self-deploy as shared devices under your tenant.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1173">若要利用自我部署，设备必须使用 USB-C 到以太网在安装的第一个屏幕期间连接到网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1173">To take advantage of self-deployment, the device must connect to a network during the first screen in setup by using a USB-C-to-Ethernet.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1174">用户启动 Autopilot 自我部署过程后，该过程将完成以下步骤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1174">After a user starts the Autopilot self-deploying process, the process completes the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1175">将设备加入Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1175">Join the device to Azure Active Directory (Azure AD).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1176">使用 Azure AD 将设备注册到 Microsoft Intune (或其他 MDM 服务) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1176">Use Azure AD to enroll the device in Microsoft Intune (or another MDM service).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1177">下载设备目标策略、证书和网络配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1177">Download the device-targeted policies, certificates, and networking profiles.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1178">预配设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1178">Provision the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1179">向用户显示登录屏幕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1179">Present the sign-in screen to the user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1180">有关详细信息，请Windows [Autopilot for HoloLens 2指南](hololens2-autopilot.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1180">Learn more from the [Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 evaluation guide](hololens2-autopilot.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1181">*立即联系帐户管理员以加入 AutoPilot 预览版。Autopilot 就绪设备即将开始交付。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1181">*Contact your Account Manager to join the AutoPilot preview now. Autopilot-ready devices will begin shipping soon.*</span></span>

### <a name="fido2-security-key-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1182">FIDO2 安全密钥支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1182">FIDO2 security key support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1183">某些用户与HoloLens或学校环境中的用户共享设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1183">Some users share a HoloLens device with others in a work or school environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1184">因此，用户可以轻松地无需键入长用户名和密码，这一点很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1184">So it's important that users can easily without typing long user names and passwords.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1185">使用 Fast Identity Online (FIDO) ，组织 (Azure AD 租户) 无需输入用户名或密码即可HoloLens无缝登录到 HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1185">Fast Identity Online (FIDO) lets anyone in your organization (Azure AD tenant) seamlessly sign-in to HoloLens without entering a user name or password.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1186">FIDO2 安全密钥是基于标准的"不可加密"无密码身份验证方法，可以采用任何外形要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1186">FIDO2 security keys are an "unphishable" standards-based passwordless authentication method that can come in any form factor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1187">FIDO 是无密码身份验证的开放标准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1187">FIDO is an open standard for passwordless authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1188">它允许用户和组织在没有用户名或密码的情况下登录到其资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1188">It allows users and organizations to sign in to their resources without a user name or password.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1189">而是使用内置于设备的外部安全密钥或平台密钥。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1189">Instead they use an external security key or a platform key built into a device.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1190">若要开始，请参阅 [启用无密码安全密钥登录](/azure/active-directory/authentication/howto-authentication-passwordless-security-key)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1190">To get started, see [Enable passwordless security key sign-in](/azure/active-directory/authentication/howto-authentication-passwordless-security-key).</span></span>

### <a name="improved-mdm-enrollment-via-provisioning-package"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1191">通过预配包改进了 MDM 注册</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1191">Improved MDM enrollment via provisioning package</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1192">通过预配包，HoloLens配置文件设置配置，而不是通过HoloLens体验进行配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1192">Provisioning packages let you set HoloLens configuration through a config file rather than through the HoloLens out-of-box experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1193">以前，预配包必须复制到内部HoloLens上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1193">Previously, provisioning packages had to be copied onto the HoloLens internal memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1194">现在，它们可以位于 USB 驱动器上，因此可以更轻松地在多个设备HoloLens重复使用，并且你可以并行预配设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1194">Now they can be on a USB drive so they're easier to reuse on multiple HoloLens devices and you can provision devices in parallel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1195">预配包现在还支持在设备管理中注册字段，因此预配后无需手动设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1195">Provisioning packages now also support a field to enroll in device management so there's no manual setup after provisioning.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1196">试试看：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1196">To try it out:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1197">将最新版本的 Windows 配置设计器从 Windows 存储下载到电脑上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1197">Download the latest version of the Windows Configuration Designer from the Windows store onto your PC.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1198">选择 **"预配HoloLens**  >  **设备预配HoloLens 2设备"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1198">Select **Provision HoloLens Devices** > **Provision HoloLens 2 devices**.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1199">生成配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1199">Build your configuration profile.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1200">然后将创建的所有文件复制到 USB-C 存储设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1200">Then copy all files that were created to a USB-C storage device.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1201">将 USB-C 设备插入任何新刷入的HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1201">Plug the USB-C device into any freshly flashed HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1202">然后按 **音量关闭**  +  **电源** 按钮以应用预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1202">Then press the **volume down** + **power** buttons to apply your provisioning package.</span></span>

### <a name="line-of-business-application-install-status"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1203">业务线应用程序安装状态</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1203">Line-of-business application install status</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1204">业务线应用的 MDM 应用部署和管理对于HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1204">MDM app deployment and management for line of business apps is critical to HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1205">管理员和用户需要查看应用安装状态，以便进行审核和诊断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1205">Admins and users need to view app install status for auditing and diagnosis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1206">在此版本中，我们在"帐户访问工作或设置"单击帐户信息"中添加  >    >    >  **了**  >  **更多详细信息**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1206">In this release, we added more details in **Settings** > **Accounts** > **Access work or school** > **Click on your account** > **Info**.</span></span>

### <a name="additional-csps-and-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1207">其他 CSP 和策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1207">Additional CSPs and policies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1208">CSP [ (配置) ](/windows/client-management/mdm/configuration-service-provider-reference?redirectedfrom=MSDN) 是一个接口，用于读取、设置、修改或删除设备的配置设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1208">A [configuration service provider (CSP)](/windows/client-management/mdm/configuration-service-provider-reference?redirectedfrom=MSDN) is an interface to read, set, modify, or delete configuration settings on a device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1209">在此版本中，我们添加了对更多策略的支持，以提高管理员对已部署设备HoloLens控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1209">In this release, we add support for more policies to increase the control administrators have over deployed HoloLens devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1210">有关云解决方案提供商支持的 CSP HoloLens，请参阅[NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1210">For the list of CSPs supported by HoloLens, see [NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1211">本版本中的新主题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1211">New in this release:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1212">**策略云解决方案提供商**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1212">**Policy CSP**</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1213">策略配置服务提供程序使企业能够在设备Windows策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1213">The Policy configuration service provider enables the enterprise to configure policies on Windows devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1214">在此版本中，我们为 HoloLens添加了新策略，此处列出了这些策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1214">In this release, we added new policies for HoloLens, which are listed here.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1215">若要了解有关详细信息，请参阅[由 HoloLens 2 支持的策略HOLOLENS 2。](/windows/client-management/mdm/policies-supported-by-hololens2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1215">To learn more, see [Policy CSPs supported by HoloLens 2](/windows/client-management/mdm/policies-supported-by-hololens2).</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1216">LetAppsAccessCamera_ForceAllowTheseApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1216">LetAppsAccessCamera_ForceAllowTheseApps</span></span>

### <a name="expanded-usb-ethernet-support-for-5glte-tethered-devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1231">扩展了对 5G/LTS 网络设备的 USB 以太网支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1231">Expanded USB Ethernet support for 5G/LTE tethered devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1232">添加了支持，允许某些移动宽带设备（例如 5G/Wi-Fi和 Wi-Fi 热点）通过 USB 连接到 HoloLens 2设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1232">Support was added to enable certain mobile broadband devices, such as 5G/LTE phones and Wi-Fi hotspots, when they're tethered to the HoloLens 2 via USB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1233">这些设备现在在网络设置 **中显示为** 另一个以太网连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1233">These devices are now displayed in **network settings** as another Ethernet connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1234"> (不支持需要外部驱动程序的移动宽带设备。) 此功能在 Wi-Fi 不可用且 Wi-Fi Tethering 性能不足时启用高带宽连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1234">(Mobile broadband devices that require an external driver aren't supported.) This functionality enables high-bandwidth connections when Wi-Fi is not available and Wi-Fi tethering isn't performant enough.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1235">若要详细了解支持的 USB 设备，请参阅 连接[蓝牙 和 USB-C 设备](hololens-connect-devices.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1235">To learn more about supported USB devices, see [Connect to Bluetooth and USB-C devices](hololens-connect-devices.md).</span></span>  

### <a name="hand-tracking-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1236">手部跟踪改进</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1236">Hand tracking improvements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1237">此版本包括多项手动跟踪改进：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1237">This release includes several hand tracking improvements:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1238">**指向姿势稳定性：** 现在，当手指被手指遮挡时，系统可以抵御手指的滑动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1238">**Pointing pose stability:** The system now resists bending the index finger when it gets occluded by the palm.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1239">此更改提高了按下按钮、键入、滚动内容等时的准确性！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1239">This change improves the accuracy when you push buttons, type, scroll content, and more!</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1240">**减少了意外的敲击：** 改进了对敲击手势的检测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1240">**Reduced accidental air taps:** We improved detection of the air tap gesture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1241">现在，在多种常见情况下（例如，将手放在一边时）中的意外激活更少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1241">There are now fewer accidental activations in several common scenarios, such as when you drop your hands to your sides.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1242">**用户交换机可靠性：** 现在，共享设备时，系统在更新手部大小时速度更快且更可靠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1242">**User switch reliability:** The system is now faster and more reliable at updating the hand size when you share a device.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1243">**减少手部窃取：** 改进了传感器视图超过两手的情况的处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1243">**Reduced hand stealing:** We improved handling of cases where there are more than two hands in view of the sensors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1244">如果多人在一起工作，现在跟踪手从用户"跳转"到场景中其他人手的可能性要低得多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1244">If multiple people are working close together, there's now a much lower chance that the tracked hand will "jump" from the user to the hand of someone else in the scene.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1245">**系统可靠性：** 修复了在设备负载较高时导致手部跟踪停止工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1245">**System reliability:** Fixed an issue that caused hand tracking to stop working when the device is under high load.</span></span>

### <a name="cortana-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1266">Cortana更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1266">Cortana updates</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1267">更新后的应用与 Microsoft 365 集成，以帮助你跨设备完成更多操作 (当前仅US-English设备) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1267">The updated app integrates with Microsoft 365 to help you get more done across your devices (currently in US-English only).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1268">在HoloLens 2，Cortana不再支持某些特定于设备的命令，例如调整卷或重启。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1268">On HoloLens 2, Cortana no longer supports certain device-specific commands, like adjusting volume or restarting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1269">新的系统语音命令现在支持这些选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1269">These options are now supported by the new system voice commands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1270">在我们的博客 中[Cortana应用。](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2020/02/28/cortana-in-the-upcoming-windows-10-release-focused-on-your-productivity-with-enhanced-security-and-privacy/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1270">Learn more about the new Cortana app in our [blog](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2020/02/28/cortana-in-the-upcoming-windows-10-release-focused-on-your-productivity-with-enhanced-security-and-privacy/).</span></span>

### <a name="quality-improvements-and-fixes"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1271">质量改进和修复</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1271">Quality improvements and fixes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1272">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1272">Improvements and fixes also in the update:</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1273">引入了主动显示校准系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1273">Introduced an active display calibration system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1274">此功能可提高全息影像的稳定性和对齐方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1274">This feature improves the stability and alignment of holograms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1275">现在，当你将头部从一侧移到另一侧时，它们就位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1275">They now stay in place when you move your head from side to side.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1276">修复了一个 bug，Wi-Fi流式HoloLens定期中断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1276">Fixed a bug where Wi-Fi streaming to HoloLens got disrupted periodically.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1277">如果应用程序指示它需要低延迟流式处理，请通过调用 [SetSocketMediaStreamingMode](/windows/win32/api/socketapi/nf-socketapi-setsocketmediastreamingmode)函数 来实现修复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1277">If an application indicates that it needs low latency streaming, implement the fix by calling the [SetSocketMediaStreamingMode function](/windows/win32/api/socketapi/nf-socketapi-setsocketmediastreamingmode).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1278">修复了在研究模式下流式传输期间发生的设备挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1278">Fixed a device hang that occurred during streaming in research mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1279">修复了以下 bug：在某些情况下，恢复会话时不会在登录屏幕上显示正确的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1279">Fixed a bug where in some cases the right user wouldn't be displayed on the sign-in screen when resuming a session.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1280">修复了用户无法通过 设置 导出 MDM **日志的问题**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1280">Fixed an issue where users couldn't export MDM logs through **Settings**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1281">修复了以下问题：在开箱即用设置后立即进行眼动跟踪的准确性可能低于预期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1281">Fixed an issue where the accuracy of eye tracking immediately following out-of-box setup could be lower than expected.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1282">修复了在某些情况下眼动跟踪子系统无法初始化或执行校准的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1282">Fixed an issue where the eye tracking subsystem failed to initialize or perform calibration under certain conditions.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1283">修复了提示已校准用户进行眼部校准的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1283">Fixed an issue where eye calibration would be prompted for an already-calibrated user.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1284">修复了驱动程序在眼部校准期间崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1284">Fixed an issue where a driver would crash during eye calibration.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1285">修复了重复按下电源按钮可能导致 60 秒系统超时和 shell 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1285">Fixed an issue where repeated power button presses could cause a 60-second system timeout and shell crash.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1286">改进了深度缓冲区的稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1286">Improved stability for depth buffers.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1287">在" **共享** "按钮反馈中心以便用户可以更轻松地共享反馈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1287">Added a **Share** button in the Feedback Hub so users can more easily share feedback.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1288">修复了 RoboRaid wan 未正确安装的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1288">Fixed a bug where RoboRaid wan't installed correctly.</span></span>

### <a name="known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1289">已知问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1289">Known issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1290">zh-CN 系统语言的问题阻止语音命令捕获混合现实或显示设备 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1290">An issue with the zh-CN system language prevents voice commands from taking a mixed reality capture or displaying the device IP address.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1291">问题要求在启动设备Cortana"Hey Cortana"语音激活后启动应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1291">An issue requires you to launch the Cortana app after starting the device to use "Hey Cortana" voice activation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1292">如果从 18362 版本更新，则还可以在"启动"中看到以前版本的 Cortana 应用的第二个应用 **磁贴**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1292">If you updated from a 18362 build, you may also see a second app tile for the previous version of the Cortana app that no longer works in **Start**.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---may-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1293">Windows全息版 1903 - 2020 年 5 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1293">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - May 2020 Update</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1295">此每月质量更新不包含任何值得注意的更改，因为团队正在处理全息Windows 2004 年 5 月更新，如前文所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1295">This monthly quality update doesn't contain any notable changes because the team was working on the Windows Holographic version 2004 May Update, as described earlier.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---april-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1296">Windows全息版 1903 - 2020 年 4 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1296">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - April 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1297">内部版本 18362.1059</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1297">Build 18362.1059</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1298">**受支持应用的深色模式**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1298">**Dark mode for supported apps**</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1299">许多Windows应用同时支持深色和浅色模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1299">Many Windows apps support both dark and light mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1300">HoloLens 2客户现在可以为支持这两种配色方案的应用选择默认模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1300">HoloLens 2 customers can now choose the default mode for apps that support both color schemes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1301">根据客户反馈，我们将默认应用模式设置为"深色"，但你随时可以轻松更改此设置：导航到 **设置 > System > Colors** 以查找"选择默认应用模式"。 </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1301">Based on customer feedback, we set the default app mode to "dark," but you can easily change this setting at any time: Navigate to **Settings > System > Colors** to find **"Choose your default app mode."**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1313">**更新中的改进和修复：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1313">**Improvements and fixes also in the update:**</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---february-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1324">Windows全息版 1903 - 2020 年 2 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1324">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - February 2020 Update</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1327">暂时禁用了 Unity 应用程序的 HolographicSpace.UserPresence API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1327">Temporarily disabled the HolographicSpace.UserPresence API for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1328">此更改可避免在视器翻转时导致某些应用暂停的问题，即使启用了"在后台运行"设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1328">This change avoids an issue that caused some apps to pause when the visor was flipped up, even if the "run in the background" setting was enabled.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1329">修复了手动跟踪导致的随机 HUP 崩溃，其中用户注意到 UI 冻结，然后在几秒钟后返回到 shell。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1329">Fixed a random HUP crash caused by hand tracking, in which the user noticed a UI freeze then back to shell after several seconds.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1330">改进了手部跟踪，以便当你用手指触摸时，该手指的上半部分不太可能意外地卷曲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1330">Improved hand tracking so that when you poke with your index finger, the upper part of that finger is less likely to curl unexpectedly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="cbae1-1331">改进了头部跟踪、空间映射和其他运行时的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cbae1-1331">Improved reliability of head tracking, spatial mapping, and other runtimes.</span></span>
